Later, the Taiwanese claimed that Fang's son was first beaten and arrested, and Fang was also beaten and injured. They did not agree to the conditions and the matter is still at a standstill. (6th Special Dispatch)

Trend of Increase or Decrease in Cultivated Land Area in China in the Last Sixty Years

The Central Agricultural Experimental Institute of the Ministry of Agriculture in Nanjing published the following trend of increase or decrease in cultivated land area in China in the last sixty years: Taking the twelfth year of Tongzhi of the Qing Dynasty as the fixed base year, up to the twenty-third year of the Republic of China, the cultivated land area increased by 1%. If calculated according to the base year of migration, the cultivated land area also increased by 1% from the twelfth year of Tongzhi to the nineteenth year of Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty. From the second year of the Republic of China to the twenty-second year of the Republic of China, the cultivated land area remained unchanged. As for the percentage of land distribution form in the twenty-third year, the average number of mu cultivated by each farmer was 210.2, wasteland accounted for 19.1% of the total land area, arable wasteland accounted for 33.3%, and arable wasteland accounted for 6.36% of the total land area. (6th Central News Agency Telegram)

Registration of Banner Lands in Beijing 34

In Nanjing, the banner lands in this city are lands leased by the garrisoned soldiers of the former Qing Eight Banners. The government has issued lease certificates over the years and collected rent annually. Transfer is only permitted, sale is not. Now, the banner lands have been transferred from the Banner People's Livelihood Office to the city government for management. The ownership should be public. Land registration will be carried out, dividing into six types: ownership, surface rights, perpetual tenancy rights, easement rights, pawn rights, and mortgage rights. Houses will be included in surface rights, and cultivated land and house sites will be included in perpetual tenancy rights, with their original names annotated. The city government has approved this plan to be implemented. (6th Dispatch)

The Judicial Yuan's Interpretation of

The Case of Dividing Boundary Lines 41

Nanjing, the Executive Yuan believes that the Judicial Yuan's interpretation of whether people can appeal in the case of dividing boundary lines is still doubtful and requests further interpretation. The Judicial Yuan's answer: The so-called administrative disposition that changes the original state of people's land refers to the new construction of ditches, roads, or embankments on people's land due to the division of boundaries. However, administrative disposition is not limited to changing the original state of the land. For example, if the water conservancy of Village A is assigned to Village B due to the division of village boundaries, causing damage to the people of Village A, then although the original state of the land has not been changed, it is an administrative disposition. The villagers who have suffered losses can file an appeal against it. A corresponding consultation is given for reference. (6th Dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

The Prerequisite for Guaranteeing the Affairs Officials Ting 42

Recently, the National Government approved the request of the Examination Yuan and instructed the directly subordinate agencies, roughly stating that affairs officials should not advance or retreat with political officials, and that qualified civil servants should not be dismissed without reason, so that they can serve the public with peace of mind and improve administrative efficiency. In addition to ordering the Legislative Yuan to draft the Civil Servant Guarantee Law, it should be followed uniformly, etc. We often feel that the corruption of our country's officialdom is half due to the careless selection of civil servants and half due to improper promotion and demotion. Therefore, fortunately, there is the support of powerful people, who can rise from the ground and soar straight up. Otherwise, even if there is extraordinary talent, they are mostly confined under the carriage and cannot fully display their talents, or even have the risk of being eliminated at any time. As a result, most high-ranking personnel hold the mentality of a five-day magistrate. The unscrupulous ones also think that it is difficult to hunt for an official position, and it is not easy to stay in office. Why not take this opportunity to search as much as possible, so as to make plans for a comeback after stepping down? The affairs personnel in lower positions are transferred with the advancement and retreat of their superiors. Since individuals have no guarantee of life, how can they arouse their interest in being loyal to their duties? The National Government, in view of this, had already issued an order to the whole country on March 1, 17th year, saying, "Recently, it has been found that various agencies often change their affairs officials with the change of political officials, not only far-reaching plans cannot be implemented, but also daily affairs are often suspended as a result. In the future, affairs officials should not be changed with political officials." On March 6, 20th year, another order was issued, saying, "Various agencies should not arbitrarily change or dismiss qualified incumbent civil servants who have been screened. This is for the sake of emphasizing selection and evaluation and eliminating opportunistic advancement. If various agencies need to reduce staff or change their organization and need to reduce staff, they should also distinguish the merits, qualifications, and length of service of each member as the standard for staying or leaving." If these two orders can be carried out vigorously and resolutely, the foundation of the modern examination and evaluation system can be laid down half of the time. Now that it is necessary to reiterate the previous orders in fact, we must have a more resolute determination to carry them out.

We have no way of guessing what the content of the Civil Servant Guarantee Law to be drafted by the Legislative Yuan will be. However, we believe that the biggest problem why affairs officials today do not have sufficient guarantees is that in fact, there are only passively prohibiting the arbitrary replacement of civil servants, and there are no actively punishing those who illegally appoint private individuals or exclude dissidents. Therefore, if the government sincerely wants to correct the long-standing malpractices, the first thing it should do is to impose sanctions on such illegal actions. According to the 198th meeting of the Central Political Conference and the third plenary meeting of the Third Central Executive Committee, all officials who must be appointed by the Political Conference or the State Council are political officials.

Appointed, recommended, and simple appointed personnel are affairs officials. The dismissal or other disciplinary sanctions of affairs officials shall be strictly in accordance with Article 2 and Article 15 of the Civil Servant Disciplinary Act, that is, affairs officials shall not be subject to dismissal, demotion, etc., unless they (1) violate the law, (2) neglect their duties, or other acts of dereliction of duty. The disciplinary agency shall also copy the original impeachment documents to the affairs officials who are subject to disciplinary action and designate a period for them to submit a written statement of defense. If necessary, they may also be ordered to attend the court for questioning. In the future, if political officials arbitrarily deprive their subordinate affairs officials of their positions or reduce their ranks and salaries without following this law and its prescribed procedures, they themselves are illegal. The Control Yuan should immediately file an impeachment case and evidence and send it to the Supervisory Committee of the Central Party Department or the National Government for disciplinary action according to their status. Only then can the status of affairs officials be fully guaranteed, and administrative efficiency can be greatly improved. Mussolini Laval Agrees on Central European Pact

Still Based on Maintaining Austria's Independence and Inviting Neighboring Countries to Participate African Issues Still Under Discussion 43

Rome, Foreign Minister Laval and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini have reached an agreement on the Central European Pact after talks here today. It stipulates that if any country interferes with Austria's independence, France and Italy will consult with each other and invite all countries bordering Austria, including Germany, to sign a non-interference protocol. The full text of the treaty between France and Italy and a request for Romania and Poland to participate in the non-interference protocol. The two countries and other countries bordering Austria should mutually agree not to interfere in each other's internal affairs, not to initiate any acts of aggression, and not to assist the activities of any terrorist groups. After the full text of the agreement is approved by the French and Italian parties, it will be notified to the German government. It is expected that Germany will be invited to join the Central European Pact in the near future. It is reported that the United Kingdom is very willing to support the final resolution, as expressed in the friendly telegram sent by Foreign Minister Simon, but it does not seem to join the agreement,

After the French Foreign Minister and the Italian Prime Minister held their first talks, they met with Italian Deputy Prime Minister Suvich in the hotel at 5 pm. The French Foreign Minister told the visiting journalists that everything was proceeding smoothly. The talks with Mussolini this morning involved everything in the treaty.

The main difficulties that the French and Italian authorities must solve now are how to discuss with the German government and to what extent should Germany be invited to participate in the non-interference protocol. Another difficulty is the integration of the interests of the three countries of France, Italy and Argentina. Since the Uruel dispute between Italy and Argentina, this matter has been particularly difficult. However, today, the Italian King declared to the Argentine ambassador his willingness to be friendly and willing to make a peaceful understanding of the Uruel dispute. The situation has greatly improved as a result.

According to a Reuters telegram from Berlin, officials are not lightly speaking about the agreement reached by France and Italy. However, a government spokesman said regarding the non-interference in Austria's independence that many countries have already made practical statements to protect Austria's independence. This kind of agreement seems to weaken rather than strengthen the importance of the declarations of various countries, and is enough to cause the impression that the United Kingdom is not involved in the agreement. Regarding the proposal for a common agreement of non-interference, the spokesman also said that Berlin believes that this document involving Austria is too late to be issued as far as Germany is concerned, because Germany has tried its best to avoid any events that interfere with Austria, etc.

When the French Foreign Minister went to the Venice Palace to participate in Mussolini's banquet today, he delivered a speech on the spot, saying that peace is still in danger, but we have great hope and should not be discouraged. France should be concerned about its own security and also know how to participate in the integration of the opinions of various countries. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini once warned mankind in the new era of Italian history not to allow humanity to retreat into the dark ages, which is understood by many countries, etc. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini then declared that Italy and France are not only working together to manage bilateral agreements, but also will promote the common doctrine of the two countries. Italy and France are not seeking to deny the friendship between the countries of Central Europe, but are actually trying to reconcile the interests and needs of the countries and move towards the path of peace. Finally, he said that there is no problem of excluding any country. During the banquet, the French Foreign Minister presented the Italian Prime Minister with the Grand Cross of Honor, and the Italian Prime Minister also presented the French Foreign Minister with the Grand Cross of Saint Mauritius and Lazarus. The French Foreign Minister also participated in the reception of the French Embassy at 6:30 pm today. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Rome, this morning, French Foreign Minister Laval and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini continued to talk for three hours. It is believed that what they discussed was mostly colonial issues, especially the acquisition of the status of Italian nationals in Tunisia and the construction of railways in Somalia. The talks were very friendly. Experts are now studying the pending cases and will present the results of their research to the French Foreign Minister and the Italian Prime Minister when the talks resume on Monday. (6th Reuters Dispatch)

Rome, the negotiations between Italy and France are still ongoing. Regarding the signing of an agreement to protect Austria's independence, Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval have reached a compromise. This agreement will be signed by France, Italy and countries whose territories are adjacent to Austria. The so-called countries with adjacent territories include the Czech Republic, Yugoslavia, Germany and Hungary. As for Romania and Poland, they will be invited to sign the agreement at a later date. As for the various issues in Africa, Italy believes that the concessions made by France are still insufficient. However, it is generally believed that a compromise can be reached tomorrow. This morning, Mussolini and Laval met for three hours. In the afternoon, French diplomats and Italian experts will complete the整理various document phrases. In the evening, French Ambassador Dang Berlan will host a banquet to welcome Laval and invite Mussolini to accompany him. It is generally believed that the talks between Laval and Mo tomorrow morning may have certain results. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Paris, Foreign Minister Laval made a speech to a Rome interviewer for the Order Newspaper, saying, "The impression I got from this negotiation in Rome is not only good, but also very good," etc. French newspapers commented on the Rome talks, saying that the situation is very good for the future cooperation between Italy and France and the advocacy of peace. For example, the Aix newspaper said that the past misunderstandings and estrangements between Italy and France can be compared to wax, and the sympathy shown by Laval and Mussolini can be compared to heat. Wax meets heat and there is no one that does not melt. This is not a miraculous miracle, but only the logic of the Latin nation's thoughts is in line with the logic, and therefore a victory is finally achieved, etc. (6th Havas Dispatch)

Rome, French Foreign Minister Laval said to people that this agreement is very good, etc. According to a Reuters dispatch from Paris, the Paris Echo and other newspapers said that Germany's opposition to joining the agreement can be eliminated, as long as the agreement is divided into two parts. One is a memorandum, which stipulates that the countries that inherit Austrian territory, namely Poland, the Czech Republic and Yugoslavia, should sign a declaration to temporarily maintain their borders and oppose foreign interference in their internal affairs. One is the French-Italian agreement, which the countries that inherit Austrian territory can participate in, stipulating that the signatory countries should consult each other when Austria's independence is endangered. Echo and other newspapers believe that Hungary, Poland and Germany, even if they do not join the French-Italian agreement, must be able to participate in this memorandum. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

Rome, Italian newspapers have published articles elaborating on the international significance of the French-Italian friendship. Among them, the semi-official "Italian Daily" said that the meeting between Laval and Mussolini was just after half a year of sudden tension in European life. Since half a year ago, the European situation has been tense, and there are many reasons for it, especially Germany's restoration of freedom of action regarding armaments. Germany's free action, rapid rearmament, and the revival of its national warlike spirit are all enough to threaten European peace. Therefore, at this time, the mutual cooperation of the major European countries is necessary, etc. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Berlin, news of the conclusion of an agreement between France and Italy in Rome has spread here, and German newspapers have shown an extremely contemptuous attitude. (6th Havas Dispatch)

London, recently, rumors have spread that Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Widger will visit London after visiting Paris. Today, Widger issued a declaration to the press, stating that Austrian cabinet members intend to meet with political leaders of Western European countries. Political figures here are very appreciative of this declaration. (5th Havas Dispatch)

London, Foreign Minister Simon telegraphed Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval today, sincerely wishing the success of the Rome talks, roughly saying that he and the British government hope that the French-Italian agreement will become a reality. At the beginning of the year, this grand event is a good sign for a more extensive understanding in Europe. (5th Havas Dispatch)

MacDonald's Speech

Optimistic about the Future of Europe 44

The League of Nations Shines Again 45

Lochy Moss, British Prime Minister MacDonald, delivered a 20-minute national radio address starting at 9:30 tonight, saying that the birth of the League of Nations was like a hastily made altar of peace, on which a faint light was placed. Sometimes the light seemed to go out. We all know that after the light goes out, the future of human civilization will be unimaginable. But tonight, we see this light shining again. However, the wind has not stopped, so the light is swaying and there is still a risk of extinction. Regarding the meeting between Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and French Foreign Minister Laval in Rome, MacDonald said that they have made us hope that this year's New Year's European peace situation can make great progress. Most of MacDonald's speech was about domestic issues, such as unemployment and housing issues. He is quite optimistic about the future of this year, saying that in all aspects, this year's commercial wages, and unemployment and other issues will be greatly improved. (5th National Telegram)

London, British Prime Minister MacDonald made a radio address on the occasion of the New Year, earnestly explaining the reasons for optimism this year to the British people. First, he stated that Britain's internal affairs are improving day by day, which is very satisfactory. Then, he assessed the international situation, roughly saying, "Our foreign work" has gradually brightened the future of peace. A peace treaty is to end the war. However, war cannot be ended only by a peace treaty, but must also rely on other means. After the peace treaty was concluded, the shrine of peace was deserted, and the only light in front of the hall was the League of Nations. However, this light also flickered, and there was a risk of extinction at any time. Now, we have finally seen the light in front of this peace hall shining again, and it is more radiant than before. Before the passing of 1934, Britain did its best for the League of Nations and peace. The Saar issue and the South Hungarian dispute were resolved with reliance on it. Now, France and Italy are conducting negotiations, and their purpose is to study how to eliminate obstacles to mutual trust. Mutual trust is the only guarantee of peace. From this point of view, will this new year open a new era for the tranquility of the European situation? MacDonald continued to mention Japan's abolition of the Washington Naval Treaty, still expressing optimism, saying that "Japan's abolition of the treaty is just issuing a notice, and it will actually take effect two years later. However, it cannot be said that it is not a serious change. But within two years, our country will never be negligent. We must find a new basis for agreement. With this new agreement, world peace can be maintained, and the arms race can also be prevented." In addition, in the history of the British Empire, 1935 will also be a memorable year. India will announce a new constitution and accept new responsibilities this year. We are willing to give it a sincere welcome. Not only that, at a time when storms are sweeping the world, Britain stands unshakable. This is what we should be glad about. Due to the differences in national conditions and the mistakes of party disputes, parliamentary politics and individual freedom are being destroyed everywhere. Only Britain's democratic politics stand alone, which is especially something we can be proud of. Three hundred years ago, the British poet Milton said, "Our English ancestors once knew how to teach their nation how to live, and future generations should not forget it." We are very fortunate to remember this golden saying today," etc. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Saito's Speech

Open Door Policy 46

New York, Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito said in a speech at the American Foreign Policy Association today that the United Kingdom and the United States should not limit Japan's navy at the same time when they have navies that can fight in Asia, making it impossible for them to fight with Europe and the United States. Because it is required that the navies of all countries should be reduced, and must be reduced to the point where they cannot attack others. Saito also carefully denied that the US government said that after Japan's naval equality, it could carry out aggression in the Far East and endanger the traditional open-door policy. He believes that Japan is not an imperialist country, just as the United States' permission for the Philippines to be independent is also abandoning its original position in the Far East. As for the oil problem in "Manchukuo", Saito believes that the protests of foreign oil companies are quite justified, saying that this matter "will be corrected". (5th National Telegram)

New York, Japanese Ambassador to the United States Saito said in a speech at the Foreign Policy Association today that the accusation that Japan has often violated the principle of the open-door policy in China in the past has been denied by the reports of US consular officials stationed abroad. If the grievances of foreign merchants are true or justified, they will be remedied. The meaning of the open-door policy is the same as commercial fairness. Saito finally said that when any problem occurs, it should be dealt with through diplomatic channels and should not be solved by naval force. (5th Reuters Dispatch)

New York, Japanese Ambassador to the United States Hiroshi Saito recently gave a speech at the Foreign Policy Association, in which he said, "The United States announced the principle of the open door in China in 1899, because at that time, the four countries of Britain, France, Russia, and Germany decided to divide spheres of influence in China and exclude Japan. At that time, the United States announced this principle in order to protect its trade with China. Since the abolition of the spheres of influence, in recent years, the so-called open-door policy has the same meaning as the equality and fairness of trade relations. Therefore, Japan's actions in China have not violated the open-door policy, and the reports of American consuls in China also deny that Japan has violated the principle of the open door. In short, various disputes regarding this issue should be resolved by diplomatic means, and should not rely on naval power as a backing," etc. (5th Havas Dispatch)

Matsuoka Will Serve as President of the South Manchurian Railway 47

According to the Nagoya Shimbun's Tokyo telephone, the establishment of an organization in Manchuria with the unity of two as its essence: a bureau for Manchurian affairs is established within the cabinet, and the Kwantung Bureau is established in Manchuria. Nagaoka is scheduled to go to Manchuria around the 10th to decide on changes in various organizations in Manchuria and the heads of Japanese officials in "Manchukuo". American Air Force Expansion 49

Another Order Placed for Eighty-Four Bombers, Navy Department to Conscript All Merchant Ships ⊙ American Hartsing

The Army Department announced today that it has placed an order with the Strongsville Aircraft Company for eighty-four bombers, totaling US$2 million. Roosevelt Advocates

Joining the World Court 50

Senate to Discuss It as Soon as Possible. Washington - It is understood from the White House meeting that President Roosevelt advocates submitting the issue of the United States joining the World Court to the Senate for discussion as soon as possible. (5th National Telegram)

Washington - The case of the United States joining the Hague International Court has been delayed for a long time and has not yet been approved. Recently, President Roosevelt has decided to listen to the leaders of the Democratic Party and request congressional approval this week. Tonight, the President held a meeting with Secretary of State Hull, Senate Democratic Leader Robinson, Chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee Thurman, and Assistant Secretary of State Sweet. The aforementioned decision was made during the meeting. At one point, Roosevelt intended to submit a special message to Congress on this issue, but he has now given up because the issue of the United States joining the League of Nations will cause fierce debate in Congress, especially in the Senate. The Democratic leaders believe that the President should devote all his efforts to the new economic recovery plan and should not personally be involved in the congressional debate on joining the League of Nations. It is also heard that someone has proposed a plan for joining the Hague International Court, containing reservations stipulating that in the event of various disputes involving the United States, the United States may reject the jurisdiction of the Hague International Court. The Senate Foreign Relations Committee will submit a report on this plan on Wednesday. (5th Havas Telegram)

Roosevelt Will Submit a

Special Message to Congress 51

Public Works and Social Policies. Washington - President Roosevelt will submit a special message to Congress next week outlining plans for public works and social policies. The proposals will contain five very important points, which even those who have previously expressed dissatisfaction with the government will acknowledge that Congress will enact into law based on the President's recommendations. The five points are as follows: (1) Allocate US$1 billion to continue existing relief efforts until the public works plan proposed by the President in his message this Friday is implemented.

(2) Pass social security legislation, including plans for old-age pensions and unemployment insurance, etc.

(3) Uphold the government's financial plan to balance government revenue and expenditure.

(4) Stop waste and avoid tax increases.

(5) Design and promote a long-term public works plan to phase out direct relief expenditures as soon as possible.

According to observers familiar with the current situation, President Luo believes that the results of last year's election have sufficiently demonstrated national trust in the government's measures. Although the major industrial circles still unanimously oppose the President's relief plan but support the adoption of an unemployment subsidy system, the general electorate supports the President's plan to provide work for all people in the country. Economic, social, and other scholars also wholeheartedly support the government because unemployment subsidies have been implemented in other countries for a long time, and their negative effects are well known. Once people receive subsidies, they stop thinking about working, and thus become a permanent burden on society. According to those close to the White House, the President does not propose to implement all of his plans immediately but wants Congress to consider the matter during this session because the state legislatures of forty-one states are meeting at this time, and Congress can also take the opportunity to discuss it with them. (5th National Telegram)

Saarland Voting Rules 52

No Slogans Allowed

No Opinions Allowed

⊙ Saarbrücken

The rules for the vote on the 13th of this month were published here today, including a clause stipulating that people must remain silent when going to the ballot box, and those who violate this will be arrested, fined, or both. Voters must not shout "Hail Hitler." People may not mention at the polling place which way they intend to vote, and must hand in their ballot papers. Voters must not express their opinions about the plebiscite. The authorities will adopt the most stringent methods to ensure the secrecy of the vote. A foreign person will be placed at each polling station to manage it. Voters must seal their ballot papers and hand them to the official, who will add another seal before placing them in the ballot box. The "German Front" and the "United Front" have been authorized by the authorities to hold an open-air rally here tomorrow, attended by 150,000 voters from all over. The final battalion of British soldiers participating in the international police force arrived here today, accompanied by 74 officers and 8 train carriages. (5th Reuters Telegram)

⊙ Saarbrücken

The first Saarland vote will be held on Monday and Tuesday, something not widely known outside the area. Since mayors, officials, and civil servants will be extremely busy on the official voting day, January 13, it has been necessary to hold the vote in advance. The voting locations for these advance votes are located in eight different places within the Saar region. (5th National Telegram)

Prince Löwenstein, a famous exile in the Saar region, was recently stripped of his German nationality by the German government. Today, the Chairman of the Saar Governing Commission ordered him to leave the country within 48 hours. Löwenstein has been very active in recent days, supporting the aims of the secessionists in many ways. Although he has obtained Czech citizenship and could have remained uninvolved in the vote, he has still attended all secessionist gatherings, advocating secession with all his might and creating a newspaper devoted to secessionist propaganda, recently reprinting an extremely anti-German article. This may be the reason the Governing Commission felt compelled to suppress him. However, the latest telegram states that Prince Löwenstein has submitted a letter of protest to the Governing Commission, and the Governing Commission has secretly agreed to allow him to continue his political activities on certain conditions. This can be confirmed by the fact that the request of German nationals to hold a demonstration was only approved on the eve of yesterday's rally, even though the request was submitted to the Commission on December 22. Soviet Union's Machine Manufacturing Industry This Year 53

Moscow - The Soviet Union's machine manufacturing industry will manufacture various machine tools worth 150 million rubles for automobile and tractor factories this year. This year, the automobile factories will have 69 new types of metal-cutting machines, 103 new types of iron-smelting furnaces, and flattening machines, all made by the Soviet Union itself. The heavy industry committee newspaper "Industrialization" stated that the speed of development of the machine tool industry in other countries in the world cannot compare with that of the Soviet Union. A few years ago, Soviet factories could only dream of using the achievements of modern machinery to manufacture automatic machine tools, flattening machines, and hammers, etc., but within two years, this technology will be completely mastered. "Today, we dare to undertake the task of supplying our own machine-made parts to new factories manufacturing automobiles and tractors. This is entirely dependent on the fact that in recent years, our country has established factories to manufacture machines and machine tools." (5th Tass Telegram)

New York - The magazine "Iron Age" here reviewed the economic situation of the past year and compared the slight increase in pig iron production in the United States with the large-scale development in the Soviet Union. The report stated that the Soviet Union's pig iron production accounted for 1% of the world's total output in 1924, and 15.6% in 1934. The Soviet Union's steel production accounted for 1.27% of the world's output in 1924, and 11.75% in 1934. (4th Tass Telegram)

Speech by the German Minister of Economy

Creditors and Raw Materials Issues 54

(National News Agency Berlin Correspondent) The German Minister of Economy and President of the National Bank, Dr. Hjalmar Schacht, recently gave a speech at the opening of the Leipzig Fair, detailing the various difficulties currently facing the German economic system with a frank attitude. Dr. Schacht's speech not only provided guidance to German economists but also provided explanations and warnings to creditors of various countries. Dr. Schacht particularly addressed representatives of the news media from various countries, stating, "Only by reporting news and facts with a sincere attitude can the newspaper industry develop." Dr. Schacht also stated that Germany's economic difficulties under the Treaty of Versailles not only caused Germany to lose £125 million in gold but also lost colonies and other productive land. Furthermore, Germany was forced to pay trillions of pounds in compensation. The planning of this compensation could only seek foreign debt. The distant cause and near result of today's economic panic is based on this. Now the compensation has been cancelled, but Germany must still fulfill its obligation to pay interest on the debt contracts concluded due to the need to pay compensation. Maintaining foreign debt interest can only be compensated by exports. This is an indisputable economic truth. Dr. Schacht also stated that various countries are now increasing tariffs or devaluing currency to curb German imports when Germany is strengthening its economic power. This move is tantamount to driving Germany out of the world market and not allowing it to be a customer. Germany has always been the third largest customer in the world market. Suppressing its imports is tantamount to refusing to be a customer. Therefore, other countries that supply Germany with raw materials are restricting Germany's export trade. Germany has always been a reliable merchant in the world market. Today, it can only increase its imports within the scope of its economic capabilities. According to Dr. Schacht, under any circumstances, the country will do its best to assist in the establishment of domestically produced raw materials, even if the value of manufactured goods is more expensive than those purchased from foreign countries, because economically, it is better to hire the unemployed to manufacture raw materials than to have the public fund unemployment relief. The most obvious fact is the various inventions of Germany during the European War. No matter how much capital is invested in a certain invention, it will eventually be utilized. On the other hand, regarding the raw materials of necessities, attention must be paid to trade reciprocity. In short, the trade of goods with those who previously had no commercial relationship with Germany can now be initiated due to the Trade Reciprocity Act. The German government is determined to rescue Germany from the situation of oppression, but the destructive power of financial experiments or abandonment policies has already been seen by major industrial countries.

(Note: Dr. Hjalmar Schacht has the honor of being an authority on economics and finance and is an outstanding figure in European financial circles. Whether this warning should be verified, we can confirm it in fact in the near future.)

Observations on Japan's Trade in the Past Year (Japanese Correspondence) 70

From January 1934 to mid-December of the same year, Japan's trade, the total value of exports, was 2,081,255,000 yuan, and the total value of imports was 2,176,705,000 yuan. In terms of exports, this was 291.45 million yuan more than the same period last year, and imports were 335.21 million yuan more than the same period last year. By the end of 1934, Japan's total trade volume would probably exceed 4.2 billion yuan, which is also possible. From an industrial and commercial perspective, this situation can truly be described as an unprecedented new record in the past five years. Therefore, most industrialists and businessmen are very optimistic, believing that Japan's economic future holds great promise for development.

However, amidst this thriving export situation, there is a shadow of pessimism, namely the total value of raw silk exports. From January to mid-December of last year, it was 391 million yuan, while in the same period this year, it was only 267 million yuan. In terms of the percentage of total exports, it has also fallen from 21.75% to 13.25%. This is not merely a matter of the rise and fall of commodities, but also has profound implications for Japan's industrial sector. It also has a significant impact on its entire national economy. In particular, the sustenance and prosperity of rural areas in various parts of Honshu are almost entirely dependent on silk. Furthermore, Japan's tax revenue, derived from rural areas and rural side businesses such as the silk industry, exceeds one-third of the total tax revenue. If sericulture declines chronically from now on, it is feared that more than just a portion of the rural areas will be affected. However, on the other hand, its light industry continues to develop upwards. Exports of cotton fabrics, including cotton cloth, wool crepe, and cotton yarn, totaled 526 million yuan, making them the largest export and its most effective weapon in capturing markets.

On the import side, cotton increased by 15 million yuan compared to last year, and wool increased by 9 million yuan. The increase in these two imports indicates a leap in the development of its cotton and wool textile industries, and also symbolizes that it will not only compete with Britain for the cotton textile market in the future, but also for the wool textile market. However, for the time being, it is gaining a slight advantage politically, namely that the large-scale import of Australian wool has eased Australia's antipathy towards Japan, thereby bringing Britain and Japan closer together.

In addition, what is more noteworthy is the increase in iron imports by 17 million yuan, the increase in machinery imports by 38 million yuan, and the increase in oil imports by 9 million yuan. The increase in these items is very different from the situation with cotton and wool. It is not related to industrial manufacturing, but rather a phenomenon of rapid progress in the military-industrial sector. From the prosperity of its military-industrial sector, we can infer the dangers it entails. We can also glean from this how much reality there is in the so-called maintenance of peace.

The total volume of export trade increased by 16% this year compared to last year. Except for the United States, it generally tended to increase. But what about the future? According to the observations of the Japanese economic community, it is believed that it has now reached a saturation point, and they dare not lightly be unconditionally optimistic. They are all paying considerable attention to vigilance.

Since Japan's foreign trade has developed in this way, and the world market has certain limitations, other countries, especially Britain and the United States, will naturally be hit. Therefore, they are building political barriers to engage in confrontation. For example, in 1933, Britain abolished the trade treaty with Japan in West Africa, and India also imposed special restrictions on the import of Japanese cotton textiles. A quota system for the import of foreign-made textiles was also implemented in other British colonies. Needless to say, the goal of this matter is to deal with Japan. In August of this year, the United States concluded a new trade treaty with Cuba, stipulating that American light bulbs have priority over those made by other countries, which is also a boycott of Japan.

Since Japan implemented currency devaluation, it has an advantage in the international exchange market. It is difficult for Britain and the United States to stand by and watch any longer. In the future, they may either conclude a monetary agreement to seek temporary relief, or re-establish political barriers to confront Japanese goods. Also, the "Manchurian" stone monopoly law implicitly contains military implications, and at the same time restricts the import of British and American oil. Britain has protested against this, but Japan has only evaded it. This is bound to develop into a major problem in the near future. Even if it is temporarily silenced by some means, it will eventually cause trouble, because this is not only about oil, but also hides an arms race. (December 29th)

Instructions of Chairman Chiang in Hangzhou

Thoroughly Implement the New Life 71

Aspire to Exert and Strive to Strengthen

Revive the Nation and Build the Country

Hangzhou Correspondence: Chairman Chiang attended the swearing-in ceremony of the members of the Zhejiang Provincial Government on New Year's Day of the 24th year and delivered instructions. The original text is recorded as follows: "Chairman Huang, members of the Provincial Government, heads of departments, today our Zhejiang Provincial Government members hold a swearing-in ceremony, which coincides with the New Year's Day of the 24th year of the Republic of China, which is also the anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China and the President's assumption of office in Nanjing. Our Zhejiang Provincial Government, from Chairman Huang and the members below, take office on such an important anniversary worthy of rejoicing. Of course, it has a very important significance, whether for the country, for our party, or for Zhejiang Province. Today's ceremony will leave a very important commemoration. I would like to take this rare opportunity to contribute a few words to the chairman of the provincial government and the members of the provincial government, as well as to all comrades and compatriots in Zhejiang Province.

Now it is the 24th year of the Republic of China, which means that our country has grown to 24 years old. Generally speaking, for an ordinary person, at the age of 24, they have completed their studies and must be able to stand on their own feet. It is truly the time when they are in their prime. Our country is also like this. At the age of 24, it should have grown into a new country in its prime, capable of self-reliance, striving, and being promising. Therefore, on this New Year's Day of the 24th year, everyone should take advantage of this good opportunity to renew their aspirations and strive for self-improvement. This time, when Brother Bei arrived in Hangzhou, he also accepted the invitation of the promotion association

Page 8

for guidance. Now, taking advantage of today's opportunity, I would like to tell all comrades that last year was the period of advocating and piloting the New Life Movement. Starting from today, New Year's Day, everyone should aspire to reform the old and establish the new, and thoroughly eliminate all the shortcomings in the past in life, society, politics, and all aspects. All our thoughts, words, and actions must be renewed according to the principles of the New Life Movement. a new Zhejiang that thoroughly implements the New Life, and extend it to build a truly new Republic of China. Secondly, as the central supervisor has just said, Zhejiang Province has many things that should be done and malpractices that should be eliminated. And the most important condition is that we have spirit and can practice the spirit of "doing it practically, doing it quickly, and doing it hard" that I often talk about. Therefore, there is never any progress in politics, society, and all aspects, and a truly new country has not yet been built. Zhang Weicun Will be Buried in Thousand Buddha Mountain 72

Yang Jinjian Talked About the Situation When Zhang Was Assassinated

Jinan Correspondence: Zhang Qun, a member of the Central Committee of the Kuomintang, was assassinated and died in the Jinde Association. Because the incident happened suddenly, it shocked the society. The military and police have been strictly arresting the murderers for days, and the provincial government has publicly offered a reward of 50,000 yuan in order to solve the case. However, until today (4th) evening, there is still no clue. Zhang's remains were encoffined this morning (4th) at 1:30 a.m. At 4:00 p.m., the various key people in the city went to pay their respects. Key people from the central government and other provinces and various friends also sent letters and telegrams of condolence in an endless stream. It is heard that the party, government, and social circles of Jinan intend to have Zhang's remains buried in the Thousand Buddha Mountain. The situation is recorded separately as follows:

The Situation of the Encoffining 73

Zhang's remains began to be encoffined today (4th) at 0:30 a.m.

The coffin prepared was made of oak wood. At 1:10, the body was placed in the coffin. At 1:30, the lid was closed and nailed. When encoffining, Zhang's mother, Leng, his wife, Ms. Liu Jinwen, his brother, Fu Ju, and his son, Minsheng, all personally served on the side. More than 30 staff members of the provincial party headquarters also stood beside them. Zhang's family was extremely sad, and the party members and various friends also shed tears for them.

Condolences from All Sides 74

The staff of the provincial party headquarters mourned Zhang's death extremely much. Today (4th), the office was closed for one day. All the staff members wore blue gauze on their arms. At 8:00 a.m., Li Wenzhai, a member of the Standing Committee of the Provincial Party Headquarters, and members Liu Xinwo and Huang Huatang led all the staff members to Zhang's residence on Xiaowei Sixth Road to pay their respects. Jian Guo Middle School was founded by Zhang Weicun. All the students in the school were extremely saddened when they heard the news of Zhang's death. At 9:00 a.m. on the 4th, the entire school went to Zhang's residence to pay their respects. Today (4th), the plain workshop in front of Zhang's residence and the spirit shed in front of the house have been set up. Key people came to pay their respects in an endless stream. In the morning, there was Wen Chenglie, the mayor of Jinan, and Wu Zhenzuan, the president of the High Court, on the spirit bed of Zhang Weicun. In the afternoon, there were the heads of various departments, Cao Fulin, the commander of the 29th Division, and Wang Shiqi, the director of the Public Security Bureau. At 4:00 p.m., in addition to the family members and party members, most of the leaders from all walks of life also participated. There were many wreaths and couplets, which were extremely honorable. Han Fuju sent representative Ma Qianli to participate in the condolence ceremony.

Funeral Staff 75

Zhang Weicun's funeral office has now been established, with Director Li Tianni, Cao Junfeng, Li Wenzhai, General Affairs Li Boqing, Hu Yusong, Yang Guangzhen, Reception Huang Lou, Zhang Heheng, Zhang Xiangdong, Hao Jiahua, Li Shuchen, Su Shougui, Liu Guanjun, Li Yujia, Liu Shouting, Liu Qianruo, Wang Xinghe, Sun Zhuomin, Wang Shihe, Huang Jie, Wang Xianfu, Inner Cabinet Pan Liuting, Zhu Xiaoching, Zhu Xiaoshan, Lu Xuexun, Outer Cabinet Wang Yuhan, Sun Youran, Lu Bing'an, Liu Guogan, Lin Yuemu, Liu Zifu, Documents Qin Xiangcun, Zhao Jixun, Liu Shuangqiao, Guo Pengxiao, Han Xuwu, Wang Dashen, Lu Baoguang, Kong Zhujiu, Wang Lianxi,

Party Headquarters Report 76

The Shandong Provincial Party Affairs Executive Committee reported to Chairman Chiang and the Central Party Headquarters after Zhang Weicun was assassinated. The telegrams are as follows: (1) Nanjing Central Party Headquarters, our Standing Committee member Zhang Weicun was shot and killed by reactionary elements at the Tiden Lantern Festival on Kewan at 7:00 p.m. We report this first. Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters Seal. (2) Hangzhou Probing Chairman Chiang, our Standing Committee member Zhang Weicun was shot and killed by reactionary elements at the Jinde Association at 7:30 p.m. on Kewan while guiding the New Life Movement Lantern Festival. We report this first. Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters Seal.

The Course of the Disaster 77

When Zhang Weicun was assassinated in the Jinde Association, his follower, Yang Jinjian, was also shot twice, one in the back of the left arm, which entered and exited from the front well, and one grazed his shoulder. He was sent to Jinan Hospital for treatment that night. After being given a heart stimulant, he was out of danger. All the circumstances of Zhang Weicun's assassination at that time have been roughly described by Yang Jinjian, but the details are not clear. In order to understand the detailed circumstances at that time, the reporter visited Yang at Jinan Hospital at 2:00 p.m. today (4th) and learned that Yang was living in Room 14 of the First Ward in the hospital, lying on a copper bed under the west wall, with his head south and feet north, covered with a blue woolen blanket, his face pale, and his spirit not yet recovered. His left arm was wrapped in white cloth and could not be moved, making it difficult to turn over. When the reporter entered, Yang slightly nodded his head on the bed. When Yang spoke, his voice was extremely low and he closed his eyes from time to time, thinking about what happened at that time. According to Yang, "The night of the 2nd was the second day of the New Life Movement Lantern Parade. Zhang Weiyuan was responsible for guiding it. After eating at the mansion at 5:00 p.m., Zhang Weiyuan went to the Party Headquarters, and Zhang Weiyuan urged the people at the Party Headquarters to quickly go to the Huangting Gymnasium to gather. At 5:45, Zhang Weiyuan and I went to Huangting again. At this time, the lights of various agencies had been prepared and gathered. After Zhang Weiyuan gave a speech, Zhang Weiyuan and I started to arrange things at the Jinde Association. The original plan was to go to Ximen Street, but because there were so many people with lanterns, we changed to Nannen and went straight to the Jinde Association on Qima Road. When we arrived at the entrance of the Jinde Association, Zhang Weiyuan walked into the gate and followed the gravel path to the south, passing the billiard room and going south until before the Peking Opera stage. Zhang Weiyuan stood on the slope where the memorial week was held every Monday and looked around. About five minutes, Zhang Weiyuan's location of the assassination at the Jinde Association, near the Kongsheng Pavilion, then walked from the billiard room to the northeast path. At that time, Zhang Weiyuan was in front and I was behind, only two or three steps apart. After passing the children's playground, we followed the path to the north. When we arrived at the side of the Kongsheng Pavilion, the people playing with lanterns and the people walking on stilts were all on the west side. The lights were bright and the noise was loud, but the area around the Kongsheng Pavilion was extremely quiet. There were no tourists and there were small pine trees on both sides. The shadows of the lights were dim, making it feel even more quiet. At this time, Zhang Weiyuan planned to pass through the golf course and go to the committee room, because Zhang Weiyuan's route was always like this every time he went to the Jinde Association, which had become a habit. Unexpectedly, at this moment, the murderer opened fire from behind. Three shots were fired in a row. The first shot hit me in the shoulder, and I fell down. Although I felt a pain in my shoulder that went straight to my heart, I knew it was not good in my heart. I got up from the ground and took two or three steps to the east, planning to pull out my gun. At this time, the murderer had fired four or five shots. When I was shot for the first time, Zhang Weiyuan looked back, and the second shot hit Zhang Weiyuan in the head. At that time, Zhang Weiyuan fell to the ground. At this time, my pistol had already been pulled out, but I could not pull the bolt because my body was paralyzed. When I turned my head, the assassin had run west into the pine forest. I shouted that there was an assassin, but because the noise was loud, no one responded. I ran to the gate. When I ran to the gate, I saw the Public Security Bureau law enforcement team. I said that Zhang Weiyuan had been assassinated and that the door should be guarded. At this time, it was only five or six minutes. Because I had been shot in the shoulder and ran for a long time, I could not walk at that time. The Public Security Bureau sent me to Jinan Hospital. Recalling that there were three murderers at the time, the one who assassinated me was a tall man in an ash-gray gown and a felt hat. The other two were short. At that time, the tall one was in front and the short ones were behind. The tall man was very quick. He shot me first, a total of three shots. I was shot twice, and the missing shot hit Zhang Weiyuan in the head. Usually, I don't pay attention to whether anyone is following me. There were too many people that night, so it was even more impossible to keep track of them. Zhang Weiyuan usually carried a gun, and he was carrying a gun that night, but because the incident happened suddenly, the first shot hit the vital point, so there was no time to pull out the gun. Moreover, the murderer came from behind. After shooting, he ran west. Because the left side of the Peacock Pavilion is full of pine trees that are as tall as a person, the murderer ran into the pine forest and could not be seen. At that time, the people playing with lanterns in the west were drumming and the tourists were like ants. I think the murderer must have mixed into the crowd and took the opportunity to escape," he said.

Yang Jinjian is 26 years old, from Zaoqiang County, Hebei Province. He has been following Zhang Weicun for more than a year. His mother is old, his father is dead, and he has two brothers. The eldest brother, Yang Jinting, is a farmer in his hometown of Zaoqiang, and the second brother, Yang Jinshan, is working in the Jiangyin County Government in Jiangsu Province. (4th)

Zhang Weicun's Family from Left to Right 78

(1) Zhang's wife (2) Zhang's son, Minsheng (3) Zhang's mother, Leng (4) Zhang's younger brother, Fu Ju

After the Severe Disaster in Northern Jiangxi

Agricultural Product Prices Plummet 79

Farmers Endure Pain and Sell at Reduced Prices

Refugees Gather in Xun City Awaiting Relief

Jiujiang Correspondence: The half of northern Jiangxi centered on Jiujiang has suffered severe drought and floods in the past, resulting in this tragic desolation. Now the famine has not abated slightly, the production of various items has decreased, and agricultural products and their by-products have increased in price due to insufficient supply. This is a natural principle, but it is now completely wrong. Except for the price of rice in Jiujiang City, which is 12.23 yuan per load, the items that come to the market from the countryside for sale are cheaper than expected. For example, chickens are ten catties per yuan, cabbage is ten texts per catty, and eggs, which were previously hindered by foreign-made products, were as low as 20 or 25 texts each. Pork is more than six catties per yuan, and retail is only 640 texts per catty. Ducks are also only one dime per catty. Prices are so cheap that it is almost suspected that there is overproduction, peace of mind for the people, and abundance of goods. In fact, it is because the rural areas have gone bankrupt. They only have to sell everything in their homes at a reduced price to make up for the loss. For example, piglets that are not full of dozens of catties and chicks that are not more than half a catty are also brought to be sold in order to exchange for a small amount of rice, or to pay rent or pay off debts. After selling everything, they often abandon their homes and flee the famine, wandering in foreign lands, only to fill the ditches. When the reporter took the China Merchants Jianghua ship from Nanjing to Xun the other day, many of the refugees who squeezed onto the ship along the way were haggard-looking. The refugees from the four villages of Jiujiang City who came to Xun Wharf to beg for food also gathered in Xun Wharf. Although the authorities sent people to block them from entering at the important intersections on the one hand, and set up shelters to accommodate them as much as possible on the other hand, the refugees begging for food on the streets are still rampant, carrying men and holding women, hungry and cold. The situation is very tragic. According to locals, along the Jiang River near the China Merchants Wharf in Xun Wharf, refugees, beggars, and vagrants who sleep in the open air must freeze to death three or four people every night. The authorities and local charities are now working hard to provide relief to this item, but I am afraid that a drop in the bucket will still not help. (4th)

Jiangsu Province Rectifies Lake Fields 80

The First Phase of the Clearing Plan is Approved

Zhenjiang Correspondence: In order to continue to thoroughly clear the mature lake fields reclaimed by the people in the counties along Taihu Lake in this province, the Jiangsu Provincial Government abolished the Taihu Lake Field Bureau and established the Taihu Lake Field Clearing Office, and approved the first phase of the clearing method, which is divided into four items: registration, surveying, payment, and issuance of licenses. The details are recorded as follows:

Registration 81

1. All reclamation households and grain households who have reclaimed mature lake fields must apply to the Clearing Office for registration within one month from the date of announcement, and they are allowed to report and receive them with priority. 2. Lake fields without grain should first be given to the original reclamation households to receive them. If there are lake fields with grain that are measured and found to have exceeded the amount of grain-free lake fields, the excess acres should first be given to the grain owners to pay the price and receive them. However, if the grain owners have not paid the embankment labor fees, they should compensate the reclamation households for the embankment labor fees of five yuan per acre. 3. If the reclamation households and grain owners do not comply with the order to register within the stipulated time limit, they should first be given to the current tenant farmers to receive them. 4. If the reclamation households, grain owners, and tenant farmers do not comply with the order to register and pay within the stipulated time limit, the Clearing Office may issue a notice for auction. 5. The reclamation households, grain owners, or tenant farmers should submit the location, acres, and boundaries of the reclaimed lake fields to the Clearing Office for registration. Each household that reports for receipt should pay a deposit of one yuan per acre, and the Clearing Office will issue a receipt. When the case is decided and the license is issued, it can be used as a抵 within the正价 that should be paid, and the receipt will be cancelled.

Surveying 82

1. After the Clearing Office receives the registration application from the lake people, it should immediately assign a surveying team to survey each location one by one. 2. The surveying team should draw a detailed map based on the surveying results. 3. Three copies of the map should be drawn for each case, one copy attached to the license, one copy kept at the office, and one copy submitted to the office for future reference. 4. The location, boundaries, acres, name of the boundary marker, date of measurement, and name of the surveyor should be indicated on the map. 5. The calculation of length and area should be in accordance with the regulations of the measurement and law promulgated by the National Government. All lake fields that are mixed with grain should be presented with the grain string for the last five years and other documents at the time of reporting, so that they can be verified and划除. If there is no grain string document to be presented, it should be regarded as grain-free and pay the price for放领. After the lake fields with grain are registered and surveyed, the Clearing Office will issue a升科知照单 and advise the county to升科, so as to重赋政.

Payment of Price 83

1. The price shall be paid according to the classification of lake fields and grades: Grade A, fish ponds, mulberry gardens, fruit gardens, and high-lying areas: eight yuan per mu; low-lying areas: six yuan per mu. Grade B, rice paddies and water fields: four yuan per mu. However, when reclamation households or tenant farmers undertake the lease, an additional 20% shall be charged based on the above prices.

2. When undertaking the lease of lake fields, in addition to paying the regular price as stipulated, a handling fee of 5% of the regular price according to the regulations of the register, a surveying fee of 5% (to be equally disbursed by the Office and the Department), and one jiao per mu shall be paid.

3. Households that report for the lease of lake fields shall pay the regular and additional prices and fees in full within one month after receiving the surveying notice.

4. If a lessee who reports for the lease of lake fields is financially constrained, they shall be allowed to pay the price in three equal installments, with each installment lasting two months. However, an additional 5% shall be charged on each installment paid.

5. If a lessee fails to pay the regular and additional prices and fees in full after six months, the bureau shall issue a certificate based on the amount of money already paid and the corresponding area of land. The remaining land shall be re-advertised for sale. If the price is not paid at all, all of the land shall be auctioned off separately.

Issuance of Certificates 84

1. If a lessee pays all the prices and fees payable in one lump sum, the clearing office shall issue a printed receipt, fill out a payment certificate, and submit it to the Finance Department for the issuance of a license.

2. If a lessee pays the prices and fees payable in installments, the clearing office shall issue a printed receipt for each installment. The payment certificate shall be filled out again on the date of full payment and submitted to the Department for the issuance of a license.

3. The clearing office shall remit all the collected prices and fees to the treasury on a daily basis and report them to the Department. The Finance Department shall allocate half of the regular price payable to the Taihu Water Conservancy Commission.

4. The Finance Department shall verify and fill out the provincial certificate, which shall be transferred by the office to the practitioner, and shall promptly notify the county government to increase the grain tax. (6th)

Revised by the Anhui Provincial Government

Collection of Relief Grain Types 85

Limited to Daily Food

Anqing Correspondence: In the past, due to the severe drought in various counties of Anhui Province this year, the Anhui Provincial Government specially set up offices for collecting relief grain in Dashengguan, Wuhu, Bengbu, Guxian, Chenjiaqian, Dingbu and other places, and established branches in Anqing, Huayang, Tianchang, Jiangba and other places. Recently, the Executive Yuan ordered the Anhui Provincial Government to close all of them by the end of the 23rd year. The Anhui Provincial Government still considered that the disaster situation in various counties was too serious and the amount of relief grain collected was insufficient, and requested a postponement of the cancellation. However, the Dashengguan branch was strongly opposed by the Beijing Municipal Government and has now been moved to Xiliang Mountain in Anhui Province to continue the collection. At the moment, the provincial government is considering the types of relief grain to be collected in various places, which originally included black and white sesame seeds, peanuts, sunflower seeds, melon seeds, and ten kinds of beans such as green, black, tea, mud, dried, yuan, silkworm, red, flat, and rice beans. It has repeatedly requested exemption from collection, and the Nanchang Provisional Headquarters has instructed that the collection of relief grain should be limited to food that can be directly used as daily meals for the people, and shall not be collected at a discounted price or distributed after price changes. Other miscellaneous grains that cannot be used as daily food and have very low yields shall also be removed and exempted from collection. A separate list of relief grain types to be collected shall be prepared and submitted for approval, etc. The matter has been raised at the 258th talk meeting of the provincial government, and it was resolved that peanuts and other categories should be exempted from the collection of relief grain. The types of grain that will continue to be collected as before and those that will be exempted are listed below. (1) To continue to collect: rice, glutinous rice, broken rice, paddy rice, glutinous paddy rice, wheat, barley, buckwheat, millet, sorghum, six-grain rice, six-grain millet, soybeans, mung beans. (2) Exempted from collection: green beans, black beans, tea beans, yuan beans, dried beans, mud beans, silkworm beans, red beans, flat beans, black and white sesame seeds, rapeseed, peanuts, peanut kernels, rice beans, sunflower seeds, melon seeds. (4th)

Hubei Province This Year

Production and Construction Plan 86

Coal, Cotton, Tung Oil, and Yarn are Listed as the Four Major Policies

The Construction Department Decides to Raise One Million Yuan to Handle

Hankou Correspondence: In the past two years, all construction in Hubei Province has focused on transportation, and highways and telephones have been largely completed. Starting this year, further efforts will be made in production and construction. The authorities of the Construction Department are currently formulating a plan to improve coal, cotton, tung oil, and yarn as the four major policies, and have decided to raise one million yuan to handle them. A brief account is given below:

Coal 87

The coal-producing areas of this province include Wuchang, Puchi, Daye, Yangxin, Nanzhang, Yuan'an, Changyang, Zigui, Xingshan, Badong, and other counties. The coal in Dexi at the border between Zigui and Xingshan is of superior quality and abundant quantity, and is known as the Xiangxi Coal System in the domestic mining industry. The recoverable output has as many as eight layers, with a total thickness of eight meters and a length of 50 kilometers. Its quality is very strong in cohesiveness after burning and is rich in coking properties. The usual method of coking can be divided into two types: non-by-product coking and by-product coking. The non-by-product coking method cannot obtain other by-products besides coke, such as in Liuhegou, Pingxiang, Zhongxing, and Kaiyuan, etc. The by-product coking method can obtain coal gas, gasoline, sulfuric acid, and nickel, etc. in addition to coke. The by-product coking method is further divided into high-temperature distillation and low-temperature distillation. The coking in Jingxing is based on the high-temperature distillation method, mainly for producing iron and steel, and gasoline is a by-product. This province is rich in iron sand in Xiangbishan, which can be used to coke with Xiangxi coal using the high-temperature distillation method, and engage in the steel industry. However, there are many places in the country where coke is produced, and the steel industry cannot be established with a small amount of capital. Moreover, several layers of Xiangxi coal have a high content of volatile matter. It has now been decided to adopt the low-temperature coal coking method, with the extraction of by-products such as gasoline as the main purpose. The semi-coke produced can be used as household fuel, which is more suitable and economical than the briquettes sold in Wuhan. In addition to gasoline, machine oil, fertilizer powder, and asphalt can also be extracted, which is very beneficial.

Cotton 88

This province's cotton production ranks second in the country. However, ignorant merchants tend to mix water and adulterate it, resulting in a loss of credibility and farmers and merchants are in distress. It is now planned to set up 20 to 50 ginning and baling factories in the cotton-producing areas of Xianghua and the upper reaches of the Yangtze River to centrally control ginning and baling. The ginning machine will be a saw-tooth ginning machine, and the baling machine will be a new-style Shanghai double-box wooden machine, which can bale four bales weighing 250 catties per hour. The baled bales must be small in volume to prevent moisture and adulteration. The fiber grades will be further distinguished to facilitate the purchase of yarn mills. It will also cooperate with the Commodity Inspection Bureau to jointly handle origin inspection and be responsible for transportation. It can be directly transported to Jiujiang, Wuhu, Shanghai, and other places, eliminating the trouble of temporary delays and re-packaging in Hankou, so that the cotton industry can be developed to seek rural revitalization.

Tung 89

Tung oil is one of China's special products. In the past, the value of exports was quite large. However, in recent years, the United States has imitated the manufacture of tung oil with considerable success, causing China's tung oil to be severely hit in the international market. Recently, Japan has also been encouraging cultivation in Korea, and the export of tung oil will inevitably be more affected in the future. As for the national tung oil production, 80 to 90 percent are exported from Hankou to foreign countries. According to the commodity inspection bureau's investigation of tung oil exports in the past three years, it was 937,707 dan in the 19th year, 606,712 dan in the 20th year, and 476,3663 dan in the 21st year, showing a decreasing trend year by year. There are about 20 counties in the Jiangxiang basins and southern Hubei Province that are suitable for planting tung trees. In March and April last year, the Construction Department planted 7 dan of tung oil seeds in Jun County, Caodian, and Shihua Street, obtaining 800 to 900 tung trees, with a survival rate of 90 percent. In order to increase production and save foreign trade, it has been decided to concentrate on afforestation in Jingshan or Jingmen on a large scale this spring. While using tractors to reclaim wasteland, animal husbandry will also be carried out to make it a group farm.

Yarn 90

This province's cotton production also ranks second in the whole country, so it is suitable for operating yarn mills. Wuhan currently has five mills: Shenxin, Taian, First, Yuhua, and Minsheng. However, the official yarn bureau run by the province has long been discontinued. It has now been decided to move the machinery of the yarn bureau to the Fancheng area for operation. First, it is close to the cotton-producing area, and the raw materials can be transported without trouble. Second, the products can be sold nearby in Henan and Shaanxi, which is more convenient than concentrating in Wuhan. (4th)

Songjiang 91

A Male Corpse Found Dead on the Road in Xiang Santu

Yesterday, a male corpse was suddenly found dead on the road in Zhou Agen's shed in Xiang Santu, east of Huayang Bridge in this city. He was wearing a peaked cap, worn-out military uniform, and was barefoot. He was about 30 years old. It is not known why he died. The Xiang police of the district reported to Xu Zhen's chief Chunpu, who in turn reported to the county court. This morning, Prosecutor Du was commissioned to go to the countryside for an examination. It was found that there were no injuries. The Xiang police were ordered to collect a coffin and place the body in it, and a notice was posted to solicit the relatives of the deceased to claim the coffin for verification.

The President of the Court Has a Definite Date for Taking Office 92

Wang Sixian, the President of the County Court of this county, has been ordered to be promoted to the President of the Nantong County Court. Yang Litang has been appointed to succeed him. According to reports, Mr. Yang has served as a prosecutor of the Supreme Court and a president of the County Court. It is said that he will come to Songjiang to take office around the 15th.
