Joint Through Traffic on Jiangnan Highways to be Held Regularly 184

The Shanghai-Wuxi Road Project is scheduled to be completed by the end of March.

Construction of the station will begin, and traffic will open in mid-April.

The Dagong Agency reports that the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department's Highway Administration originally planned to hold a joint through traffic ceremony for the Jiangnan Highway on October 10th last year. However, due to insufficient preparations and the incomplete construction of several roads such as the Wuxi-Shanghai Road, it could not be implemented. Now, Chairman Chiang has ordered the construction authorities of the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Nanjing, and Shanghai to expedite the completion of highway construction to facilitate transportation. After receiving the order, Shen Baixian, the Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department, instructed the Highway Administration to complete the main and branch lines of the Jiangnan Highway by the end of March, and plans to officially hold the joint through traffic ceremony for the Jiangnan Highway on April 1st. The route will depart from Wuxi, pass through Jiangyin, Wujin, Zhenjiang, Jurong, Nanjing, Liyang, Yixing, and return to Wuxi. Then, it will pass through Changshu, Wujiang, Jiaxing, Pinghu, Zhapu, Shanghai, Liuhang, Baoshan, Wusong, the city center, and then disperse to Baoshan Road in Zhabei. Along the way, the long-distance bus stations in each location will be responsible for providing fuel and water, as well as relief services, and the military and police stationed in the area will be responsible for protection. The vehicles will be jointly provided by various long-distance bus companies.

Completion of Shanghai-Wuxi Highway Expected Soon 185

The Shanghai-Wuxi Highway, which stretches across Jiangnan and is built along the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway, has seen active construction since the Jiangsu Construction Department began supervising the project in sections from April 20th last year. Of the 149 bridges on the entire line, 89 within the Wuxi to Taicang section have been fully completed. Approximately 70% to 80% of the 60 bridges along the Taicang-Jiading and Jiading-Shanghai sections have also been completed. Furthermore, more than 40 of the 66 culverts on the entire line have been completed. The entire road surface, with crushed brick and crushed stone as the base, has also been laid for approximately 90%. It is expected that the project can be completed in another two months, and the entire project should be completed around March.

Long-Distance Buses to Begin Service Soon 186

The Shanghai-Wuxi Road Long-Distance Bus Company held its inaugural meeting on October 12th last year and elected Mr. Wang Xiaolai as the General Manager. Mr. Wang has repeatedly inspected the project along the route and the station construction plan to facilitate passenger boarding and alighting. Currently, there are more than 30 towns and cities between Wuxi and Shanghai. Each town will have a station, and other villages will have stop points. It is currently scheduled to start constructing stations next month, and it is expected to be completed in early April. It will only take about two hours to travel from Shanghai to Wuxi. It is expected that through traffic can be implemented in mid-April.

Shanghai Telegraph Bureau Ordered to Begin Business Inspections 187

Five Measures to be Implemented on January 1st

To Encourage Telegraph Personnel to Increase Efficiency

The Ministry of Transportation has formulated five measures for inspecting telegram receiving and dispatching offices to encourage telegraph personnel and improve work efficiency, which will be implemented from January 1st of this year. The measures are as follows: (1) Telegraph bureaus with separate receiving and dispatching offices should conduct inspections at any time in accordance with these measures; (2) For the aforementioned inspection affairs, bureaus with business inspectors will assign inspectors to conduct inspections from the business section chief and business chief at any time, with at least two inspections per office per month. Bureaus without business inspectors will be handled by the business chief. The business section chief or business chief should also conduct one inspection per office per month. If necessary, the director or chief engineer should also personally conduct inspections; (3) Inspection personnel should pay attention to the following points when inspecting receiving and dispatching offices: A. Whether employees are late or leave early, or arbitrarily leave their posts; B. Whether there is private unauthorized substitution; C. Whether each receiver and dispatcher is competent for receiving and dispatching work, and whether the receiver and dispatcher understand various receiving and dispatching regulations; D. Whether staff members have violated various rules of the receiving and dispatching office; E. Whether the current received telegram fees match the numbers listed in the flow; F. Whether there is encroachment on public telephone call fees, or allowing acquaintances to make free calls; G. Other matters that should be noted; (4) Inspection personnel should fill out an inspection report form detailing the situation of each receiving and dispatching office inspected, and submit it to the responsible person for review. The format of the inspection report form will be determined separately; (5) These measures will be implemented from January 1st, 1935.

Record of the Provisional Representative Meeting of the Liji Church Association 194

The Shanghai Liji Church Association held a provisional representative meeting yesterday, with more than 200 people attending. The reasons for this are several, the most important of which is that the seating arrangements for the leaders of various public halls and altars have not been reformed in a unified manner. The case was discussed, and it was decided that the leaders of various public halls should follow the government's instructions to reform in a unified manner. Those who violate this will be dealt with in accordance with the Social Bureau's No. 1066 order of the 18th year of the Republic. All other points were obeyed, and the leadership of Chairman Zhang was followed. This representative meeting dispatched representatives Zhang Wenlin, Wang Kechang, Jiang Changyong, Cai Xueshi, Liu Jinfan, Yu Shouhuan, etc. to represent all Liji Church comrades in the city to request reinstatement. This was unanimously approved. The rest is omitted.

Mr. Lu Shoulian has been engaged in the automobile business for nine years. Recently, due to the heavy workload, he resigned from his position at Meitong Company at the end of the year. It happened that the Xintong Automobile Company on Foch Road lacked someone to manage it. Upon hearing the news of Mr. Lu's resignation, friends repeatedly requested him to take the position of Chinese Manager. Although Mr. Lu felt that he was busy with affairs and difficult to manage, he finally agreed to take office at Xintong Company today due to the inability to refuse the request. Recently, it has merged with Buick Company to expand its business, specializing in the sale of famous automobiles such as Cadillac, Buick, Chevrolet, LaSalle, Wackerho, etc., which are popular everywhere. In addition, Mr. Lu has traveled to the United States for many years and has extensive social connections in Shanghai. It is expected that with the launch of the new plan, these cars will definitely sell well. This is also good news in the automobile industry this year.

Record of the Shanghai Machine and Plumbing Industry Association Meeting 197

Encourage Fellow Traders to Help Disaster Victims

The Shanghai Machine and Plumbing Industry Association held its 9th meeting at its meeting hall at 5:00 PM yesterday. Nine committee members including Ni Zhanghe and Wang Xinsong were present, and Lu Yunhu and others attended as observers. Pan Zhiliang was the chairman and Qin Boyan was the recorder. Following the usual ceremonies: A. The chairman's report briefly stated: 1. Disaster victims are everywhere in the country and urgently need relief; 2. The hazards of earth and water to human health should be prevented and controlled; 3. Plans to set up a cooperative to help the market, etc. B. Discussion: 1. Members reported difficulties in purchasing water from Xiecheng. How should we respond? Decision: The association will negotiate with Xiecheng members. 2. How to deal with members who have not paid membership fees? Decision: Send personnel to persuade and collect fees. 3. Luo Shouxian has promised to pay membership fees, but has not paid them yet. How should we respond? Decision: Send Tang Abing, Zhang Xiu, and Wang Xinsong to contact them again. If there is no result, seek other solutions. 4. Is it appropriate to establish a cooperative? Decision: Draft the articles of association first and then make a decision. 5. Unclean earth and water are harmful to the health of Chinese and Westerners. How should we find a solution? Decision: Investigate and then submit it to the authorities for inspection or prohibition. 6. Notify all fellow traders to donate money to help disaster victims. 7. Inspect water tanks to increase hygiene. Decision: Send personnel to investigate secretly and request the authorities to handle it. After the meeting, the meeting adjourned. The association's letter to fellow traders for disaster relief is recorded below: Although we who are engaged in business in Shanghai can still make a living amidst the current economic depression, we must look back at the rural areas in the interior. The economic bankruptcy is severe in many places, which is unbearable. The disaster victims in the disaster areas eat tree bark and grass roots to fill their hunger. Who in Shanghai can know this kind of misery? The severe winter is approaching, and the disaster victims still have no cotton clothes to wear, waiting for people to rescue them. People in Shanghai are donating money to help. We fellow traders are also Chinese citizens. How can we sit idly by and not save the disaster victims who are crying out for food? Therefore, this association is specifically requesting all fellow traders to find a way to donate some money to help disaster victims based on their charitable conscience. Saving a life increases blessings and longevity. For payment of donations, please go directly to the Urgent Relief Association for handling. Please all fellow traders in Shanghai rise up to help disaster relief!

After the Storm at Qilu University Subsides

Li Zhifan Reports on the Future Direction of the University

(Jinan Correspondence) Since the board meeting held last year, Qilu University in this city has hired Mei Yibao as president. Before Mei arrived, Vice Chairman Li Zhifan was temporarily appointed as acting president. Because Chairman Kong Xiangxi did not agree to take office, Li was also considering the matter of acting president and delayed for a long time. No one was responsible for university affairs. Recently, Zhu Youru, a director of the university, passed through Jinan from Beijing on his way to Beiping. According to reports, Kong has agreed to take office as chairman, so Li has also agreed to assume the position of president. Students welcomed Li's announcement. Classes resumed on the 4th, and the Qilu University storm has come to an end. On the 4th, Li Zhifan went to the Department of Education to report on the beginning and end of his acting presidency and the future direction of the university, asking the department for guidance. He also inquired about how to receive the 5,000 yuan that the provincial government assists the university with each year. Director He Siyuan and Chief Secretary Wang Jinxin received him, and the main points of the conversation were as follows: (1) Consolidate the foundation of the school. Li said that Qilu University's 500,000 yuan in funding all came from donations from foreign churches. However, the nature of the donations may not be sustainable in the long term. If it is interrupted, the university's affairs will be suspended. The point about consolidating the foundation of the school is very important. In the future, he plans to first organize an alumni association. More than 1,000 people have graduated from Qilu University over the years and are scattered throughout the country. He wants to organize them, protect the alma mater, and appoint responsible committee members. If each person contributes a minimum of 50 yuan per year, then there will be 50,000 yuan, which is a small supplement. In addition, the university's construction committee has also decided to improve the board of directors, limiting the number of directors to 15, with 10 Chinese and 5 foreigners, according to the regulations of the Ministry of Education, to be responsible for running the university, so as to avoid being scattered and disorganized.

(2) The school goes to the countryside. The current government's education methods focus on the countryside, and the general opinion is also the same. Furthermore, the foreign church that is responsible for Qilu University's funding holds two meetings each year. Recently, it also stated that spending a large sum of 500,000 to 600,000 yuan each year to run an ordinary university is not very meaningful and advocated that the school go to the countryside. Due to these various relationships, Qilu University's future direction will follow this trend, but there is absolutely no plan to change the College of Arts and Sciences into a rural normal school. Students heard this rumor and became uneasy, repeatedly questioning the school. The school has made a clear statement that the future direction of the school will focus on the countryside, but there is absolutely no plan to change the College of Arts and Sciences into a normal school.

(3) Make up for the school's deficit. Before President Mei Yibao arrives at the school, Li's term as acting president will be half a year, calculated until the end of the academic year on June 23rd of this year. The school's deficit is about 40,000 yuan. Fortunately, this number is not very large and does not seem to be a problem. Moreover, the Qilu University Construction Committee has also decided to find ways to assist the school's finances, and it may not be difficult to raise 40,000 yuan.

(4) The problem of the Dean of the College of Arts and Sciences. After Li agreed to take the position of acting president, he sent a letter to President Mei Yibao to report. Mei replied, saying that he would submit his resignation from the position of president of Mingxian College in Taigu at the upcoming board meeting and may come to Jinan during the summer vacation. Currently, the only problem is Lin Jiqing, the Dean of the College of Arts and Sciences. Acting President Li hopes that Lin will return to the school to take office. The students have also sent Lin a telegram welcoming him. However, Lin has not yet expressed his opinion. Lin's contract as Dean of the College of Arts and Sciences was for five years and expired in March of last year. If Lin is to be rehired, another five-year contract must be signed. However, Li's term as acting president is only half a year, and he is afraid to hire a dean of the College of Arts and Sciences with a five-year term, so he has consulted with Mei Yibao. There has not yet been a reply. It is likely that the school can rehire him, but he is not sure whether Lin will agree to take office. The Department of Education reported to the Ministry of Education that the students of the College of Arts and Sciences have already started classes and that someone is responsible for the president's duties. The department specifically telegraphed the Ministry of Education to report the situation. Also, on the afternoon of the 4th, Li Zhifan convened a meeting of all faculty and staff of the College of Arts, Sciences, and Medicine to discuss the direction of progress.

High School Outstanding Student Fellowship Movement

Youth Problem Discussion Held Yesterday 215

Discussion Problems Divided into Four Groups

Instructors Invited to Explain Separately

The High School Outstanding Student Fellowship Movement sponsored by the Shanghai Special Municipal Party Department held a youth problem discussion at the auditorium of Wuben Girls' High School yesterday. Tong Xingbai, Tai Shuangqiu, Yang Weiyu, and Zhang Yiping were invited to serve as instructors and answer questions separately. The details of each are recorded as follows:

Participating Schools 216

A total of more than 200 students from over 40 schools including Jingye, Wuben, Fudan, Nanyang, Minli, Daxia, Guanghua, Qingxin, Nangaon, Chizhi, Qingnianhui, Mailun, Fushi, Xinlu, Peiming, Tongji, Datong, Lida, Qiaoguang, Jianguo, Dongya, Zhengfeng, Xinmin, Dagong, Kaiming, Zhirenyong, Private Shanghai High School, Shanghai Kindergarten Teacher School, Hujiang, Minli Girls' High School, Huahua, Yuqing, China Vocational School, and Cihang Midwifery School attended.

Committee Member Tao Reports 217

The meeting opened at 2:00 PM. Chairman Tao Baichuan, Committee Member, received Yu Zhongbiao, Wang Longzhang, and others. The chairman first reported, stating briefly that today is the third session of the High School Outstanding Student Fellowship Movement sponsored by the Municipal Party Department. The fourth fellowship movement will not be held this semester due to examination issues. The fourth session was originally scheduled to visit the Municipal Government and pay tribute to the Wusong War Zone. If the students are willing to participate, it will be held together when the outstanding first-year high school students are received next semester. Today is a discussion meeting. Before the meeting, there will be a simple test with questions about thoughts and knowledge, which can be used as a reference for education. Due to time constraints, the speeches will be stopped. Students will first raise questions, and then the instructors will answer them.

Further Education and Reading 218

The first group is further education and reading.

The discussion question is how to enable poor students to pursue further education. Students first discussed together, followed by instructor Tai Shuangqiu's opinion, stating briefly that in his personal feelings, it is necessary for young people to contribute to the country and society in the future, and further education is of course necessary, but it is also possible without further education. Those who pursue further education do not necessarily read books, and those who read books do not necessarily pursue further education, such as Edison in the United States and Wang Yunwu of the Commercial Press in China, who have not pursued further education, which is one example. Therefore, the idea that you cannot read books without money should be corrected by aspiring young people. However, how to enable young people with economic difficulties to pursue further education should be the result of efforts in many aspects such as government, society, and education. As for the methods: (1) Mutual assistance for further education; (2) Subsidized further education. Finally, he hopes that everyone will not be discouraged and at the same time hopes that they will not think that they cannot read books without further education.

Employment and Service 219

The second group is employment and service.

The discussion question is how to enable secondary school graduates to obtain suitable jobs. Instructor Yang Weiyu gave his opinion, stating briefly that there are a total of twenty-nine questions in the employment and service group, but many are the same. When talking about this issue, it is necessary to state first that for any problem, the solution must have a scientific or educational principle, and secondly, there must be a scientific or political or educational power. However, we have neither principles nor power in today's discussion, so we cannot solve it absolutely. The above problem is not only a problem for the entire society, but also a problem for the entire nation's future. If the entire nation's future is resolved, then the problem of secondary school students' employment will not be difficult to solve. As for seeking employment, first, we must find jobs and not necessarily rely on others; (2) We cannot have vanity when looking for a job; (3) Only hard work can achieve final success. The most important thing is that when you need to find a job and cannot find one, you must not be discouraged. Seek answers from the ways of effort, opportunity, and time.

Thought and Belief 220

The third group is thought and belief.

The discussion question is how to train us to have correct core beliefs. Instructor Tong Xingbai gave his opinion, stating briefly that the issue of thought and belief is difficult to explain because the scope is too broad. In terms of time, there are advancing and retreating thoughts. In terms of nature, there are positive and negative thoughts. Moreover, thoughts are different, just like everyone's complex outlook on life. Therefore, thoughts must come from oneself in order to have core beliefs. Mr. Sun Yat-sen said it most clearly, that is, first have thought, then have belief, and then have power. Thought is the cause of belief, and belief is the result of thought. According to personal observation, the most suitable for China is the core belief of the Three Principles of the People. As for each person, please analyze and study your own thoughts before embarking on a path. Also, whether thinking about the past or the future, because the past is experience and the future is to achieve progress. The past is a reference tool, and the future is the goal of research. For core thoughts, you must grasp the present.

Love and Marriage 221

The fourth group is love and marriage.

Instructor Zhang Yiping gave his opinion, stating briefly: (1) Love is not a game. Love is a legitimate thing. Secondary school students should not be in love, but they are not opposed to love. (2) Love should be responsible. In the past, freedom of love was unknown, which has misled many young people. (3) Marriage should also consider one's own family environment. Finally, Tao Baichuan explained and supplemented each point, and then

It ended.

Xu Zeyu Talks About 222

The Education Situation in Zhejiang Province

Xu Zeyu, Secretary of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education, came to Shanghai the other day. The reporter met him at his residence in Shanghai and talked freely about the education situation in Zhejiang Province. According to him, Zhejiang's education has made great progress after several rounds of active reorganization by Jiang Menglin, Chen Bulei, Zhang Daofan, and Ye Suchong. With the existing funds, so much work is being done, and the allocation is also very appropriate. Since Director Xu took office, he has planned the administrative facilities in detail, and the content will be discussed in detail in the future. As for the current situation:

(1) Independent education funding. Three items are designated: foil business tax, tobacco and alcohol surtax, and slaughter business tax, totaling approximately 2 million yuan per year, as special education funds, which are allocated by the Department of Finance on a daily basis. This is different from the Jiangsu Province method. This matter is implemented in three phases. The first phase, foil business tax of 90,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.08 million yuan per year, was implemented in November of the 22nd year. The second phase, foil business tax of 100,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan per year, and tobacco and alcohol surtax of 200,000 yuan per year, totaling 1.4 million yuan, was implemented in July of the 23rd year. Currently, it is in the second phase, and the Department of Finance allocates 116,666 yuan of foil business tax and tobacco and alcohol surtax per month. The shortfall is found by the Department of Finance separately. From May of this year, it will be the third phase: foil tax of 100,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan per year, tobacco and alcohol surtax of 200,000 yuan, and slaughter business tax of 600,000 yuan, totaling 2 million yuan.

(2) Last year, the various counties suffered from famine, and tax revenue was greatly affected. Provincial schools were already in arrears of approximately 400,000 yuan. At the end of the year, Director Xu of the Department of Finance agreed to allocate 200,000 yuan first. The schools were about to close for the holidays, making it difficult to maintain them. As for education in various counties and cities, the total of 3.31 million yuan for 75 counties and 1 city was affected by the famine, and income is expected to decrease by more than 1.7 million yuan. Therefore, local education has fallen into a very difficult situation. Primary school teachers in various counties are owed salaries, with some being owed for as long as seven or eight months, and others for three or four months. Many primary schools have closed. It is hoped that Zhejiang merchants and all sectors of society overseas will work together to save the education of their homeland, which is on the verge of collapse. The Department of Education is currently requesting that 1 million yuan be allocated from local public bonds as an education reserve fund to help local education. This fund has not yet been received. It is also stipulated that various counties and cities should compile a tight budget for education funds and try to tighten expenditures.

(3) There are 13 provincial secondary schools, 20 county and city joint secondary schools, and 49 private secondary schools in the province. The number of students is 6,253 in provincial schools, 4,608 in county and city joint schools, and 9,699 in private schools, totaling 20,560. The funding for provincial secondary schools is more than 1 million yuan, for county and city joint schools is 220,000 plus yuan, and for private schools is more than 830,000 yuan.

(4) There are 5 provincial normal schools and 10 county joint normal schools. Various secondary schools also have attached normal departments, simple normal departments, rural normal departments, kindergarten normal departments, and infant protection normal departments, which are not included. There are 1,218 students in provincial normal schools, 849 in county joint schools, and 97 in private schools, totaling 2,164. The funding for provincial schools is more than 260,000 yuan, for county joint schools is more than 48,000 yuan, and for private schools is more than 6,000 yuan.

(5) There are 5 provincial vocational schools, 6 county joint vocational schools, and 12 private vocational schools. Various secondary schools also have attached business departments, civil engineering departments, and agricultural departments, which are not included. There are 919 students in provincial schools, 772 in county joint schools, and 1,051 in private schools, totaling 2,742. The funding for provincial schools is more than 190,000 yuan, for county joint schools is more than 47,000 yuan, and for private schools is more than 110,000 yuan.

(6) There are a total of 12,462 primary schools in the province, including 78 kindergartens, 11,046 primary schools, 1,245 elementary schools, and 93 short-term primary schools, with a total of 20,859 classes, a total of 706,201 students, and a total of 30,645 faculty and staff.

(7) The funding for social education undertakings in the province has increased year by year, and now totals 229,267 yuan, accounting for 1.02% of the total education funding. The funding for social education in counties and cities has also increased year by year, reaching 406,424 yuan in the 22nd year, accounting for 1.224% of the total education funding in counties and cities.

When Director Xu took office, the internal staff was not changed, and only four new employees were added, eliminating the bad habits of ordinary administrative agencies during the transition between new and old personnel. The previous handover funds, as reported in the news a few days ago, were more than 290,000 yuan in cash, which is inaccurate because they were all funds held in trust, such as airplane donation proceeds, which could not be used, or treasury bonds. In fact, the actual handover cash was only a few hundred yuan.

Special Column

A Retrospective on the Renaissance Week of Shanghai North High School by Tang Naikang 227

(I) Introduction

Time flies, and the year 1934 will soon become a historical date. As the New Year approaches, it is appropriate to review the past year and encourage future endeavors. Therefore, I will briefly describe the past situation of this year to seek correction from the enlightened individuals of this era.

(II) The Process of Renaissance

Since our school was destroyed in the January 28th Incident, colleagues have adhered to the principle that education is life and have vowed to revive it. We invited renowned figures from all walks of life to form a Renaissance Design Committee, which convened on March 5, 1933, at the club to discuss and plan the revival. A chairman and various officers were elected to implement the renaissance plan. Fortunately, with the enthusiastic support of the committee members and the dedicated efforts of our colleagues, after five months, the funds for rebuilding the school buildings were raised. Drawings were made and prices were estimated, and it was decided to start construction on the original site on October 21st. A groundbreaking ceremony was held on November 4th, attended by representatives from various party and government sectors who earnestly encouraged us to cultivate youth as preparation for the renaissance of the nation. In February 1934, the entire project was completed, including a classroom building, a dormitory building, and a Renaissance Hall, which can accommodate approximately 700 students. On April 8th, a dedication ceremony for the rebuilt school buildings was held, with a large number of guests attending. Mayor Wu of this city personally attended and instructed us to make spiritual education the standard for the efforts of all teachers and students. The perilous situation of the past two years of turbulence has finally entered a stable period.

(III) Overview of the Past Year

Since moving into the new school buildings, although the material facilities cannot fully meet expectations, they are still roughly complete. However, in education, the most important thing is the spirit. Here, I will divide it into four categories: academics, moral education, physical education, and student life, to observe the spiritual life of the past year.

A) Academics: Secondary school education must take into account both further education and employment. Our school strictly adheres to the standard curriculum set by the Ministry of Education and seeks truth from facts, so that students can use what they have learned to prepare for entering society and university. The following are some of the academic matters that can be mentioned in the past year:

(1) Adding Full-Time Teachers: The uneven level of students in recent years has become increasingly apparent from past grades. After careful consideration, the reason is half due to the students' lack of effort and half due to the teachers' inability to dedicate themselves fully. Therefore, this year, we have specially added full-time teachers for subjects such as English, mathematics, and science. This will not only allow teachers to concentrate their abilities but also give students more opportunities to approach them, melt away emotional barriers, and arouse students' interest in studying.

(2) Holding Subject Competitions: Subject competitions are held in stages. Those that have already been held include Chinese and mathematics, and those that will be held are English and science. Standards are set for grouping based on the level of proficiency. Prizes are awarded to the top students in each group to encourage them.

(3) Visiting Industrial Institutions: Senior students visit various industrial institutions to broaden their knowledge. Those who have visited include the Longhua Aircraft Factory, the Yabaoer Electric Bulb Company, the Kangyuan Canning Factory, the Shanghai Printing and Dyeing Company, the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, the Xinya Pharmaceutical Factory, and so on. Students are also required to write visit reports to promote the practical application of knowledge.

(4) Checking In-Class and Extracurricular Performance: In addition to holding two quizzes each semester, we also check in-class and extracurricular performance, such as composition, mathematics, English exercise books, and notes for each subject, to verify whether students are attentively listening in class and whether they are guiding and practicing diligently outside of class.

(5) Increasing Graduation Class Exams: Graduation class students can complete a stage in their academic journey. After graduation, they either continue their studies or serve the community. Increasing the number of exams provides an opportunity to review and learn new things, and it also trains the agility of thought.

(6) Connecting with Student Families: The excellence of school education depends heavily on the guidance of family education. Our school emphasizes daily assignments to avoid fostering a mentality of侥倖 (seeking luck). If a student fails a quiz, the parents are notified in the hope of helping them supervise and increase teaching efficiency.

B) Moral Education: Our school has consistently emphasized strict moral education for the past eighteen years, without indulgence or oppression, guiding students to self-governance and putting their actions on the right track. The principles and methods are briefly described below:

(1) Principles: A. Strictly adhere to the main purpose and implementation guidelines of education, to cultivate young people's national morality of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, faith, righteousness, and peace, and to cultivate courage, perseverance, and habits of discipline. B. Promote the spirit of the nation, guide the work of saving the country, encourage virtues such as love, public service, labor, and perseverance, and prevent bad habits such as selfishness, greed, romanticism, and decadence. (To be continued)

Sports News

Unexpected Harvest: Youyou Defeats Lux 228

Four to Zero: Revenge for Previous Defeat

Two Goals in Each Half

In yesterday's Western Union First Division football match between Youyou and Lux, there were approximately over one thousand spectators in Shen Garden. The result was beyond the expectations of most people, with Youyou defeating Lux by a score of four to zero, avenging their 5-2 defeat in the first week. Not only were the members of the Youyou Association overjoyed, but the thousands of spectators were also dancing with joy. Lux, who had eliminated Western Police with a score of one to zero in the second week of the Scoccimarro Cup, suffered a shutout, demonstrating the unpredictability of military affairs.

Iron Leg Opens the Scoring 229

Youyou won the kickoff and immediately took the offensive. Every player was fierce and eager to be first. After about six or seven minutes of back-and-forth play, Youyou made a stunning move, opening the opponent's net. Luo Haiguang passed the ball to Wang Nanzhen, who sprinted down the left wing and sent it to the center. Sun Jinshun happened to arrive at just the right moment and kicked the ball with great force. Kirkham tried to save it, but only managed to graze the ball.

Lux Counterattacks 230

Lux launched a counterattack. Hultbek had a beautiful diagonal shot that was saved by Zhang Rongcai. Liang Shutang mistakenly passed the ball back, but fortunately, no harm was done. Jiang Shan Jing, who was injured, rested for only a moment before returning to the field. Simmons fired a shot from the center, but Yun Fenglin touched the ball outside the free-kick line. Boseley took the free kick but missed. During these thirty minutes of Lux's counterattack, Lux's lack of coordination among the forwards ultimately led to nothing.

Wang Shusen Steals the Camp 231

Shen Baigui made two surprise attacks, and Sun Jinshun also made a solo raid, but both failed to score. In the last five minutes of the first half, Youyou's players surrounded Lux's goal. Sun and Wang attacked repeatedly, but Kirkham saved them all. The ball went from left to right. Wang Shusen watched calmly and saw an opportunity to sneak through. He made a dash and advanced through the crowd, making the score two to zero at halftime.

Youyou Uses Heavy Artillery 232

Lux kicked off in the second half. Youyou adopted a high-pressure tactic, attacking fiercely. Lux's defense was under constant bombardment, but they defended stubbornly for a long time. Sun Jinshun also made a solo penetration, but was blocked by Standiguerra. He then tried to send the ball over, but it was difficult to get in. Sweeping and charging, they still couldn't score, demonstrating the intensity of the offense and defense.

Goalkeeper Performs Well 233

Youyou's performance was better than before, especially Zhang Rongcai, who is a noteworthy goalkeeper. He has a clear head and can remain calm in chaos, which is commendable. Simmons passed to Beck, who went to the center. Kirkham shot at the goal, but it went over the bar. Zhang Rongcai made several saves during this period, earning applause and cheers. Hultbek made a sneaky attempt, getting the ball from behind, and powerfully shot at the goal, but it was saved by Rongcai again. If Hultbek hadn't made so many mistakes, Lux might not have been shut out in the second half.

Another Two Goals in a Row 234

Youyou pressed harder and harder, and scored two more goals in the last five minutes, bringing the score to a huge four to zero. Sun Jinshun got the ball from behind and made another sprint. Luo Haiguang supported him, and Lux's two defenders were distracted, allowing Sun to kick the ball in with his iron leg. In the last two minutes, General Sun came down from the sky again. Logan hurriedly chased after him, and Shen Baigui made a high shot. Logan blocked it with his hand, and Luo Haiguang kicked the penalty, gently curving the ball in. The game ended immediately after.

Little Western Heaven 244

— By Zhang Henshui

Chapter 7: Hearing Words, She Hides Tears and Sells Herself into Misery; Carefully Peering at Invitation Cards, He Earnestly Seeks Refuge

Cheng Zhiqian quickly stood up and introduced to Li Shilian, "This is Mr. Wang Beihai. He is a high school student here. He aspires to go to Beiping in the future to take the university entrance exam, so he is tutoring algebra and geometry with me. He is really diligent. He never misses any of the practice problems he learns every day, and he sends them to me every day to be corrected. Although I am very busy, I always take some time out to help such a diligent young man, so he comes to me every day. But he doesn't like to talk much, so even when he comes, no one knows." Because Cheng Zhiqian introduced him so solemnly, Li Shilian was too embarrassed not to say a few polite words, so he smiled and said, "So diligent, really rare!" As he spoke, he couldn't help but turn his gaze to Yueying and smiled, "You're here too." Yueying lowered her head, raised her eyelids, and looked at Li Shilian. As Li Shilian's gaze met hers, he chuckled. Cheng Zhiqian was very unhappy to see this, and he frowned and looked at Li Shilian, smilingly saying, "Don't make things difficult for her. Sigh! They are all pitiful creatures." Although he said this with a smile, there seemed to be a very serious attitude hidden within his smile. After all, Li Shilian didn't want to offend him over this small matter. The chairman even invites him to dinner, and the director even lends him his car to travel. So, he sat down on a square stool diagonally opposite Yueying and said with a smile, "How dare I make things difficult for this girl? I heard the tea attendant say that her happy news had moved, and when I saw her, I was reminded of this matter, so I naturally couldn't help but smile." As he spoke, he glanced at Yueying again. He was sitting with his head lowered, his feet together, and his hands supporting his knees. It was as if sitting there, the movement of his hands and feet was free. Cheng Zhiqian offered Li Shilian a cigarette, and he also smoked one to accompany him. (105)

Nanjing Governor 245

— Yi Shi

Our hometown, Yixing, has a local saying: "Nanjing Governor." The meaning of the name is very funny and a bit humorous. Every time the season reaches the cold winter, this local saying can often be heard, especially in small restaurants, where you can see people shouting "Nanjing Governor" at the top of their lungs.

Leaving my hometown and studying in Shanghai, I can also hear this local saying in small restaurants. Now that it is winter again, the "Nanjing Governor" is also on the market.

As for the meaning of the name, let me introduce it first. Because winter is a cold season, many dishes at mealtime are never eaten piping hot. Therefore, many leftover dishes are put together and cooked, adding some fresh ingredients. This is called "Governor" (the character "督" (du) is a colloquial term, meaning "to cook"). And "Governor" also means the central government, so it is called "Nanjing Governor."

Strangely enough, the "Governor" has a special flavor, both hot and delicious, and economical. It is even better than an order of combined dishes costing several yuan. Generally, people like to eat "Governor," and that is the reason.

If you are interested, prepare a few taels of white spirits and a packet of peanuts, and eat them slowly together. There is a truly indescribable flavor. Using it to pass the long nights of this harsh winter, reading the books you like, imagining the fun at this time, is like floating away to become an immortal. Ladies and gentlemen with leisure! You might as well try the taste of "Nanjing Governor," and it will certainly not disappoint you.

Tidbits 246

— (Jiaoxin)

If a woman marries a handsome man, she will definitely have "one extra layer" of anxiety, because while it is certainly gratifying to be married to a handsome man, on the one hand, she is also afraid that her husband will fall in love with someone else and lose her love. Conversely, if a woman marries an ugly husband, although she may be unhappy in her heart, she can rest assured and not have to be on guard. From this, it can be seen that there is no absolute perfection or absolute deficiency in the world.

"Taking Up for the Underdog" 247

— Rong Yu

Among the people coming and going on the road, there are always two absolutely contradictory mentalities: one is "everyone sweeps the snow in front of their own door, and does not care about the frost on other people's roofs"; the other is "when seeing injustice on the road, drawing one's knife to help." The former is called "mature and prudent," and can also be called "selfish and self-interested." As for the latter, they are mostly hot-blooded, and after being influenced by the eleventh son in the drama and the golden Arhat in the novel, they become enthusiastic people who "join in even if it is none of their business." However, compared to these two types of people, the latter always suffers, and that is what is meant by "troubles all arise from sticking one's neck out." But society cannot do without this kind of person. Now, let me give two examples!

A streetcar was crowded with people, and the ticket seller was too busy to sell tickets. There was a mischievous child hiding in the crowd, holding a copper coin in his hand, refusing to buy a ticket. After the streetcar crossed the Waibaidu Bridge, there were fewer passengers, and a ticket inspector suddenly jumped on. He found the child and insisted that the ticket seller had been skimming. The ticket seller could not explain, and his tickets were torn up, so he had to admit his bad luck. Unexpectedly, a Cheng Yaojin jumped out, and a passenger shouted injustice for the ticket seller, saying, "We are all Chinese, let's help each other." Unexpectedly, the ticket inspector darkened his face and said, "I am Korean, I don't help Chinese people." The passenger scolded him for being a slave of a conquered country, and they ended up fighting. When the streetcar arrived at the station, this passenger who had nothing to do with it ended up going to the police station with the ticket inspector.

Next to the early morning vegetable market, there are many vendors carrying loads on their shoulders and in their hands. These vendors are prohibited by the police station's regulations, so as soon as they see the shadow of the police, they quickly hide into the alleys without a trace. One day, a child selling scallions and garlic was simple-minded and was caught by the police. He赖 (lai: refuse to leave) on the ground and refused to go, crying in his mouth. Suddenly, many people gathered to watch. One onlooker couldn't bear it any longer and said to the police, "He's so pitiful, let him go!" The police shook his head and said! "It's official business!" Seeing that he didn't agree, the onlooker added, "Catching robbers is meritorious, catching a few vendors won't get you promoted to chief!" Seeing that his words were sarcastic, the police let go of the vendor and dragged the onlooker who had taken up for the underdog to the jail.

Records of Floating Fragrance from the Imperial Court 249

"Today, we are going to the hunting grounds, which can be said to be a most suitable and interesting day!" She said solemnly as usual, "We will take this opportunity to hold a memorial ceremony for our ancestors. Because on this very day, one of our ancestors, who was then only a tribal leader and not yet an emperor, but tribal conflicts were very common. This time, another conflict broke out. In the battle, our side was in a very unfavorable situation, and even our food supply was cut off. On this day, we had to divide the remaining cold rice among everyone as much as possible. But it was really too little to satisfy their hunger. Helplessly, they had to gather a lot of wild raw vegetables, mix them with the cold rice, and swallow them reluctantly to fill their stomachs. This is a general overview of the situation. If you want to know the details, wait until we get to the hunting grounds to talk about it! Because the place where this story happened is also a forest, a forest as dense and deep as the forest in the hunting grounds!"

The other half of the reason may have been because she thought there would be a new ceremony today, which she would lead us to hold, and therefore she felt very happy. The Tomb of Gui Youguang 250

— Tie Shui

Ever since reading "A Brief Account of My Late Mother," I can never forget the genuine affection revealed in the text, and the name of its author, Gui Youguang, is also deeply imprinted in my memory.

This time, I happened to be hiking in Kunshan, and with a different kind of feeling, I went to pay homage to his final resting place. The tomb is located in the northeast of Kunshan, less than half a kilometer from the bustling city, surrounded by low walls, with an area of about five or six acres, and the tomb is in the center. The size of the tomb is no different from ordinary ones, but because it has been rebuilt with cement, it looks very majestic. In front of the tomb stands a stone tablet erected in the twenty-fourth year of Qianlong, which reads "The Tomb of Mr. Gui Zhenchuan, Vice Minister of the Nanjing Court of Imperial Sacrifices of the Ming Dynasty." In addition to this, there are three newly built small pavilions in the tomb. In the small pavilion inscribed with the words "Looking Up To," two stone tablets are embedded in the wall, with inscriptions that are not very clear, probably epitaphs or something of that nature.

Gui Youguang was a native of Kunshan in the Ming Dynasty. Zhenchuan was the alias people used to call him. He was born intelligent and could write articles at the age of nine, but because he repeatedly failed the imperial examinations, he did not pass the examination until he was fifty-eight years old. He became the magistrate of Changxing County. In the year before his death, at the age of sixty-five, he was recommended by Grand Secretary Gao Gong and Zhao Zhenji to be the Vice Minister of the Nanjing Court of Imperial Sacrifices to revise the Veritable Records of Emperor Shizong, which was the most glorious period of his life.

The characteristic of his articles is that he uses true feelings to describe everyday trivial matters. His "Record of the Thinking-of-Son Pavilion," "Record of the Xiangji Pavilion," and other essays, like "A Brief Account of My Late Mother," can move every reader and make you unable to forget them. And his faithful descriptions and unpretentious language have a very modern flavor.

In Kunshan, this tomb, along with Gu Tinglin's handwritten copy of "Book on the Advantages and Disadvantages of the Provinces and Kingdoms," are known as two ancient sites that are enough to glorify Kunshan.

Travel Notes

On the Indian Ocean (Part 1) 251

— Zhang Ruogu

October 29th, departed from London for Scotland. November 1st, in Glasgow, boarded the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's new ship "Hai Zhen" and set sail. The climate in Scotland was severely cold. Looking at the snow-covered mountains from the harbor, although the cabins were equipped with hot water radiators, I still felt the chill. But after crossing the Atlantic Ocean, the weather changed suddenly, and the heat in the Mediterranean Sea, the Red Sea, and the Indian Ocean increased sharply, as if it were high summer. The electric fan in the bedroom rotated day and night, but the nights were hot and difficult to fall asleep. During the day, there was nothing to do, so I lay on the deck with disheveled hair and bare feet, wearing a single shirt and white trousers, basking in the sun and watching the sea, which was quite carefree.

There were only four passengers on the ship, including me. The other three travel companions were all doctors who had completed their studies in Belgium and were returning home in glory. We each occupied third-class cabins, and our lives were quite comfortable. The ship's cook was from Guangdong, and we ate Western food three times a day, which was quite tiresome. Sometimes the doctors cooked Chinese food themselves, which was quite delicious. The navigator (commonly known as the second mate) was Mr. Xue Bangxiang from Wuxi, a graduate of the Liverpool Nautical School. We spent our time chatting in the morning and evening, so the long fifty-day sea voyage did not feel lonely.

The "Hai Zhen" was newly completed in a British shipyard. The voyage of this maiden voyage was estimated to take forty-five days to reach Shanghai. It was originally scheduled to pass through the Suez Canal on November 14th, but in order to save coal, the ship's speed was reduced from fifteen miles per hour to about seven or eight miles. It was not until 3:00 a.m. on the 15th that it docked at Port Said on the north bank of the Suez Canal. Port Said is one of Egypt's important commercial ports, located in the middle of the three continents of Europe, Asia, and Africa, and is the only passage from Asia to Europe. It has a population of over 194,000, mostly Arabs and Egyptians. The locals of Port Said have a very bad reputation, mostly thieves, but this is not necessarily the case. It is just that good people are harmed by bad people.

The day before the ship arrived at the port, the entire ship became vigilant and declared martial law. All doors, large and small, were locked, and even the fire hoses, which were originally hung on the walls, were taken down and stored in the storage room. According to the sailors, the locals of Port Said are good swimmers and can climb onto the deck when people are unprepared to steal things. Whether it's cups, knives, forks, matches, or handkerchiefs, they will take whatever they can get their hands on, so we must take precautions in advance.

At 6:00 a.m., Egyptian peddlers climbed onto the deck to sell goods. One of them, who was fluent in Cantonese, asked Dr. V, who was traveling with us, "Do you want erotic pictures?" The asking price was two shillings. Dr. V agreed to the price, but after checking, the goods were not the original ones, only a few photos of models. It turned out that they had already "switched the baby."

At about 7:00 a.m., the east was already white, and the sun rose. Some locals boarded the ship and urged us to go ashore for sightseeing. At that time, the Egyptian and Arab coal handlers hired by the captain, twenty people in a small boat, came one after another, climbing the four boards, with ferocious faces, which made people feel scared. I was not used to the coal dust and the noise, so I asked the locals to find me a ferry. But the sailors advised against it, fearing accidents. They also warned that the locals were cunning and rogue, and even if a guest had no money on him, there was a risk of being "skinned alive." So we went ashore at about 9:00 a.m., paying one shilling each for the round trip, and hired an old guide to be our interpreter and companion during the tour.

The old guide was very honest, attentive, and sincere, which is rare to find among the locals of Port Said. Before we left, we jointly signed a letter of introduction to be used as a reliable guide for our compatriots who visit Port Said in the future.
